
### CHECK IF IDENTIFYING OBJECT LIST IS CORRECT, (RE)CREATE IT IF IT'S NOT

ec_check_identifying_object_list = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			ec_identifying_object_list_is_correct = no
		}
		ec_create_identifying_object_list = yes
	}
}

### COLLECT INFORMATION ON ARABLE RESOURCES

ec_check_arable_resources = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = ec_checked_arable_resources
				}
				has_global_variable_list = bg_wheat_farms
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_variable_list = bg_wheat_farms
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = bg_wheat_farms clear_global_variable_list = bg_rye_farms clear_global_variable_list = bg_rice_farms clear_global_variable_list = bg_maize_farms clear_global_variable_list = bg_millet_farms clear_global_variable_list = bg_livestock_ranches clear_global_variable_list = bg_cotton_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_dye_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_silk_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_banana_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_sugar_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_tea_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_coffee_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_tobacco_plantations clear_global_variable_list = bg_opium_plantations 
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = ec_checked_arable_resources
			value = 1
		}
		ec_start_arable_resources_check = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			global_var:ec_checked_arable_resources < 3
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = ARoAI_economy_events.300
			days = 2
		}
	}
}

### CALCULATE INCORPORATED POPULATION

ec_calculate_incorporated_population = {
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_incorporated_population
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_coastal_incorporated_population
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_incorporated_gdp
		value = 0
	}
	every_scope_state = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = {
					name = ec_incorporated_population
					add = prev.state_population
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ec_incorporated_gdp
					add = prev.gdp
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_coastal_incorporated_population
						add = prev.state_population
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				incorporation_progress > 0
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = {
					name = ec_incorporated_population
					add = {
						value = prev.state_population
						multiply = prev.incorporation_progress
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = ec_incorporated_gdp
					add = {
						value = prev.gdp
						multiply = prev.incorporation_progress
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_coastal_incorporated_population
						add = {
							value = prev.state_population
							multiply = prev.incorporation_progress
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### CALCULATE COUNTRY WEEKLY INCOME

ec_calculate_country_weekly_income = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = ec_previous_gold_reserves
			has_variable = ec_previous_debt
		}
		
		# From no debt to no debt
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				gold_reserves >= 0
				var:ec_previous_gold_reserves >= 0
				scaled_debt <= 0
				var:ec_previous_debt <= 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = ec_country_weekly_surplus
				value = {
					value = gold_reserves
					subtract = var:ec_previous_gold_reserves
					divide = 4.35
				}
			}
		}
		
		# From debt to debt
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				gold_reserves <= 0
				var:ec_previous_gold_reserves <= 0
				scaled_debt > 0
				var:ec_previous_debt > 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = ec_country_weekly_surplus
				value = {
					value = var:ec_previous_debt
					divide = 100
					subtract = scaled_debt
					multiply = credit
					divide = 4.35
				}
			}
		}
		
		# From debt to no debt
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				gold_reserves >= 0
				var:ec_previous_gold_reserves <= 0
				scaled_debt <= 0
				var:ec_previous_debt > 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = ec_country_weekly_surplus
				value = {
					value = var:ec_previous_debt
					divide = 100
					multiply = credit
					add = gold_reserves
					divide = 4.35
				}
			}
		}
		
		# From no debt to debt
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				gold_reserves <= 0
				var:ec_previous_gold_reserves >= 0
				scaled_debt > 0
				var:ec_previous_debt <= 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = ec_country_weekly_surplus
				value = {
					value = 0
					subtract = {
						value = credit
						multiply = scaled_debt
					}
					subtract = var:ec_previous_gold_reserves
					divide = 4.35
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Nothing of the above
		
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = ec_country_weekly_surplus
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_country_weekly_surplus
			value = weekly_net_fixed_income
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_previous_gold_reserves
		value = gold_reserves
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_previous_debt
		value = {
			value = scaled_debt
			multiply = 100
		}
	}
}

### COLLECT BUDGET COSTS SUCH AS CONSTRUCTION AND MILITARY

ec_collect_budget_costs = {
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_government_estimate
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_construction_estimate
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_military_estimate
		value = 0
	}
	every_scope_building = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_government_administration
					is_building_type = building_port
					is_building_type = building_university
				}
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = {
					name = ec_government_estimate
					subtract = prev.weekly_profit
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_building_type = building_construction_sector
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = {
					name = ec_construction_estimate
					subtract = prev.weekly_profit
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_barracks
					is_building_type = building_naval_base
				}
			}
			root = {
				change_variable = {
					name = ec_military_estimate
					subtract = prev.weekly_profit
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = ec_government_costs
				}
				var:ec_government_estimate > ec_government_costs_variable
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_government_costs
			value = var:ec_government_estimate
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = ec_construction_costs
				}
				var:ec_construction_estimate > ec_construction_costs_variable
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_construction_costs
			value = var:ec_construction_estimate
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = ec_military_costs
				}
				var:ec_military_estimate > ec_military_costs_variable
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_military_costs
			value = var:ec_military_estimate
		}
	}
	remove_variable = ec_government_estimate
	remove_variable = ec_construction_estimate
	remove_variable = ec_military_estimate
}

### CLEAR BUDGET COSTS VARIABLES

ec_clear_budget_cost_variables = {
	remove_variable = ec_government_costs
	remove_variable = ec_construction_costs
	remove_variable = ec_military_costs
}

### CHANGE TAX LEVEL AND GOVERNMENT WAGES

ec_change_budget_settings = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = ec_country_weekly_surplus
			is_player = no
		}
		
		# Budget is above neutral
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				ec_budget_health = {
					level = 0
				}
			}
			
			# Raise wages
			
			set_government_wage_level = medium
			set_military_wage_level = medium
			
			# Lower taxes
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					ec_budget_health = {
						level = 1
					}
					NOT = {
						any_scope_state = {
							has_active_building = building_conscription_center
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						tax_level = very_high
					}
					set_tax_level = high
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						tax_level = high
					}
					set_tax_level = medium
					set_government_wage_level = medium
					set_military_wage_level = medium
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						tax_level = medium
					}
					set_tax_level = low
					set_government_wage_level = medium
					set_military_wage_level = medium
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						tax_level = low
					}
					set_tax_level = very_low
					set_government_wage_level = medium
					set_military_wage_level = medium
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Budget is below neutral
		
		else = {
			
			# Lower wages
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					ec_budget_health = {
						level = -2
					}
					OR = {
						tax_level = high
						tax_level = very_high
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ec_can_cut_government_wages = yes
					}
					set_government_wage_level = low
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ec_can_cut_military_wages = yes
					}
					set_military_wage_level = low
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -2
						}
					}
					OR = {
						tax_level = high
						tax_level = very_high
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ec_can_cut_government_wages = yes
					}
					set_government_wage_level = very_low
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ec_can_cut_military_wages = yes
					}
					set_military_wage_level = very_low
				}
			}
			
			# Force military wages when in conflict
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					ec_is_using_military_forces = yes
				}
				set_military_wage_level = medium
			}
			
			# Raise taxes
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					ec_budget_health = {
						level = -3
					}
					OR = {
						tax_level = very_low
						tax_level = low
						tax_level = medium
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						tax_level = very_low
					}
					set_tax_level = low
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						tax_level = low
					}
					set_tax_level = medium
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						tax_level = medium
					}
					set_tax_level = high
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -3
						}
					}
					OR = {
						tax_level = very_low
						tax_level = low
						tax_level = medium
						tax_level = high
					}
				}
				set_tax_level = very_high
			}
		}
	}
}

### ADDITIONAL CALCULATIONS THAT ARE REQUIRED FOR SCRIPT FUNCTIONING

ec_preliminary_calculations = {
	
	# Square root of millions of incorporated population
	
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		value = {
			value = var:ec_incorporated_population
			divide = 1000000
		}
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_root
		value = 0.1
	}
	ARoAI_calculate_square_root = yes
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_square_root_of_incorporated_population
		value = var:csr_output
	}
	remove_variable = csr_output
	
	# Square root of millions of GDP
	
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		value = {
			value = gdp
			divide = 1000000
		}
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_root
		value = 0.1
	}
	ARoAI_calculate_square_root = yes
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_square_root_of_gdp
		value = var:csr_output
	}
	remove_variable = csr_output
	
	# Square root of GDP per capita
	
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		value = {
			value = gdp
			divide = {
				value = total_population
				min = 1
			}
		}
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_root
		value = 0.1
	}
	ARoAI_calculate_precise_square_root = yes
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_square_root_of_gdp_per_capita
		value = var:csr_output
	}
	remove_variable = csr_output
	
	# Square root of incorporated GDP per capita
	
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		value = {
			value = var:ec_incorporated_gdp
			divide = {
				value = var:ec_incorporated_population
				min = 1
			}
		}
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_root
		value = 0.1
	}
	ARoAI_calculate_precise_square_root = yes
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_square_root_of_incorporated_gdp_per_capita
		value = var:csr_output
	}
	remove_variable = csr_output
	
	# Square root of minus half unincorporated GDP per capita
	
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		value = {
			value = ec_gdp_minus_half_unincorporated
			divide = {
				value = ec_population_minus_half_unincorporated
				min = 1
			}
		}
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		nearest = 0.1
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_root
		value = 0.1
	}
	ARoAI_calculate_precise_square_root = yes
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_square_root_of_minus_half_unincorporated_gdp_per_capita
		value = var:csr_output
	}
	remove_variable = csr_output
	
	# Square root of construction points
	
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		value = modifier:country_construction_add
	}
	round_variable = {
		name = csr_input
		nearest = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = csr_root
		value = 1
	}
	ARoAI_calculate_square_root = yes
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_square_root_of_construction_points
		value = var:csr_output
	}
	remove_variable = csr_output
	
	# Target surplus of bureaucracy
	
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_incorporation_bureaucracy_cost
		value = 0
	}
	every_scope_state = {
		limit = {
			is_incorporated = no
			incorporation_progress <= 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				root.var:ec_incorporation_bureaucracy_cost < state_population
			}
			root = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ec_incorporation_bureaucracy_cost
					value = prev.state_population
				}
			}
		}
	}
	change_variable = {
		name = ec_incorporation_bureaucracy_cost
		divide = 5000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:ec_incorporation_bureaucracy_cost > ec_institution_bureaucracy_cost
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_surplus_bureaucracy_target
			value = var:ec_incorporation_bureaucracy_cost
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_surplus_bureaucracy_target
			value = ec_institution_bureaucracy_cost
		}
	}
	remove_variable = ec_incorporation_bureaucracy_cost
}

### UPDATE COASTLINE OF MARKET CAPITAL

ec_update_coastline_of_market_capital = {
	while = {
		limit = {
			any_in_list = {
				variable = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
				any_neighbouring_state = {
					owner = root
					is_coastal = yes
					NOT = {
						root = {
							is_target_in_variable_list = {
								name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_in_list = {
			variable = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
			every_neighbouring_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
					is_coastal = yes
					NOT = {
						root = {
							is_target_in_variable_list = {
								name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
				}
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### COLLECTING ALL THE STATE LEVEL DATA REQUIRED FOR THE SCRIPT

ec_collect_state_level_data = {
	
	# Set up country level counters of government building
	
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_government_administration_count
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_construction_sector_count
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_university_count
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_railway_count
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_port_count
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_barracks_count
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_naval_base_count
		value = 0
	}
	
	# Write free workforce into variable
	
	every_scope_state = {
		limit = {
			ec_state_has_free_workforce = yes
		}
		set_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce
	}
	
	# Collect country level excess production
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce
				percent <= 0.50
			}
		}
		set_variable = ec_check_excess_production
		ec_check_excess_production_on_country_level = yes
	}
	
	# Prepare closest coastline states of market capital
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			root.market.owner = root
		}
		root.market_capital = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			every_neighbouring_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_coastal = yes
						NOT = {
							root = {
								is_target_in_variable_list = {
									name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
									target = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
					root = {
						add_to_variable_list = {
							name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				every_neighbouring_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = root
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_coastal = yes
							NOT = {
								root = {
									is_target_in_variable_list = {
										name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
										target = prev
									}
								}
							}
						}
						root = {
							add_to_variable_list = {
								name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ec_update_coastline_of_market_capital = yes
		}
	}
	
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_lowest_infrastructure
		value = 1.00
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_lowest_tax_capacity
		value = 1.00
	}
	
	# Cycle through every state
	
	every_scope_state = {
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				root.var:ec_lowest_infrastructure > ec_infrastructure_load_percent
			}
			root = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ec_lowest_infrastructure
					value = prev.ec_infrastructure_load_percent
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				root.var:ec_lowest_tax_capacity > ec_tax_capacity_load_percent
			}
			root = {
				set_variable = {
					name = ec_lowest_tax_capacity
					value = prev.ec_tax_capacity_load_percent
				}
			}
		}
		
		#
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_coastal = yes
				NOT = {
					root = {
						is_target_in_variable_list = {
							name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					root.market.owner = root
					
					#
					
					save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_1
					NOT = {
						any_neighbouring_state = {
							NOT = {
								this = scope:ec_state_1
							}
							owner = root
							root = {
								is_target_in_variable_list = {
									name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
									target = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
					any_neighbouring_state = {
						NOT = {
							this = scope:ec_state_1
						}
						owner = root
						save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_2
						NOT = {
							any_neighbouring_state = {
								NOT = {
									this = scope:ec_state_1
								}
								owner = root
								root = {
									is_target_in_variable_list = {
										name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
										target = prev
									}
								}
							}
						}
						OR = {
							root = {
								is_target_in_variable_list = {
									name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
									target = prev
								}
							}
							any_neighbouring_state = {
								NOR = {
									this = scope:ec_state_1
									this = scope:ec_state_2
								}
								owner = root
								save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_3
								NOT = {
									any_neighbouring_state = {
										NOT = {
											this = scope:ec_state_1
										}
										owner = root
										root = {
											is_target_in_variable_list = {
												name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
												target = prev
											}
										}
									}
								}
								OR = {
									root = {
										is_target_in_variable_list = {
											name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
											target = prev
										}
									}
									any_neighbouring_state = {
										NOR = {
											this = scope:ec_state_1
											this = scope:ec_state_2
											this = scope:ec_state_3
										}
										owner = root
										save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_4
										NOT = {
											any_neighbouring_state = {
												NOT = {
													this = scope:ec_state_1
												}
												owner = root
												root = {
													is_target_in_variable_list = {
														name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
														target = prev
													}
												}
											}
										}
										OR = {
											root = {
												is_target_in_variable_list = {
													name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
													target = prev
												}
											}
											any_neighbouring_state = {
												NOR = {
													this = scope:ec_state_1
													this = scope:ec_state_2
													this = scope:ec_state_3
													this = scope:ec_state_4
												}
												owner = root
												save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_5
												NOT = {
													any_neighbouring_state = {
														NOT = {
															this = scope:ec_state_1
														}
														owner = root
														root = {
															is_target_in_variable_list = {
																name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
																target = prev
															}
														}
													}
												}
												OR = {
													root = {
														is_target_in_variable_list = {
															name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
															target = prev
														}
													}
													any_neighbouring_state = {
														NOR = {
															this = scope:ec_state_1
															this = scope:ec_state_2
															this = scope:ec_state_3
															this = scope:ec_state_4
															this = scope:ec_state_5
														}
														owner = root
														save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_6
														NOT = {
															any_neighbouring_state = {
																NOT = {
																	this = scope:ec_state_1
																}
																owner = root
																root = {
																	is_target_in_variable_list = {
																		name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
																		target = prev
																	}
																}
															}
														}
														OR = {
															root = {
																is_target_in_variable_list = {
																	name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
																	target = prev
																}
															}
															any_neighbouring_state = {
																NOR = {
																	this = scope:ec_state_1
																	this = scope:ec_state_2
																	this = scope:ec_state_3
																	this = scope:ec_state_4
																	this = scope:ec_state_5
																	this = scope:ec_state_6
																}
																owner = root
																save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_7
																NOT = {
																	any_neighbouring_state = {
																		NOT = {
																			this = scope:ec_state_1
																		}
																		owner = root
																		root = {
																			is_target_in_variable_list = {
																				name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
																				target = prev
																			}
																		}
																	}
																}
																OR = {
																	root = {
																		is_target_in_variable_list = {
																			name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
																			target = prev
																		}
																	}
																	any_neighbouring_state = {
																		NOR = {
																			this = scope:ec_state_1
																			this = scope:ec_state_2
																			this = scope:ec_state_3
																			this = scope:ec_state_4
																			this = scope:ec_state_5
																			this = scope:ec_state_6
																			this = scope:ec_state_7
																		}
																		owner = root
																		save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_8
																		NOT = {
																			any_neighbouring_state = {
																				NOT = {
																					this = scope:ec_state_1
																				}
																				owner = root
																				root = {
																					is_target_in_variable_list = {
																						name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
																						target = prev
																					}
																				}
																			}
																		}
																		OR = {
																			root = {
																				is_target_in_variable_list = {
																					name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
																					target = prev
																				}
																			}
																			any_neighbouring_state = {
																				NOR = {
																					this = scope:ec_state_1
																					this = scope:ec_state_2
																					this = scope:ec_state_3
																					this = scope:ec_state_4
																					this = scope:ec_state_5
																					this = scope:ec_state_6
																					this = scope:ec_state_7
																					this = scope:ec_state_8
																				}
																				owner = root
																				save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_9
																				NOT = {
																					any_neighbouring_state = {
																						NOT = {
																							this = scope:ec_state_1
																						}
																						owner = root
																						root = {
																							is_target_in_variable_list = {
																								name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
																								target = prev
																							}
																						}
																					}
																				}
																				OR = {
																					root = {
																						is_target_in_variable_list = {
																							name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
																							target = prev
																						}
																					}
																					any_neighbouring_state = {
																						NOR = {
																							this = scope:ec_state_1
																							this = scope:ec_state_2
																							this = scope:ec_state_3
																							this = scope:ec_state_4
																							this = scope:ec_state_5
																							this = scope:ec_state_6
																							this = scope:ec_state_7
																							this = scope:ec_state_8
																							this = scope:ec_state_9
																						}
																						owner = root
																						NOT = {
																							any_neighbouring_state = {
																								NOT = {
																									this = scope:ec_state_1
																								}
																								owner = root
																								root = {
																									is_target_in_variable_list = {
																										name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
																										target = prev
																									}
																								}
																							}
																						}
																						OR = {
																							root = {
																								is_target_in_variable_list = {
																									name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
																									target = prev
																								}
																							}
																						}
																					}
																				}
																			}
																		}
																	}
																}
															}
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
						target = prev
					}
					ec_update_coastline_of_market_capital = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
						target = prev
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_building = building_port
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_1
							any_neighbouring_state = {
								NOT = {
									this = scope:ec_state_1
								}
								save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_2
								owner = root
								OR = {
									has_building = building_port
									any_neighbouring_state = {
										NOR = {
											this = scope:ec_state_1
											this = scope:ec_state_2
										}
										save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_3
										owner = root
										OR = {
											has_building = building_port
											any_neighbouring_state = {
												NOR = {
													this = scope:ec_state_1
													this = scope:ec_state_2
													this = scope:ec_state_3
												}
												save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_4
												owner = root
												OR = {
													has_building = building_port
													any_neighbouring_state = {
														NOR = {
															this = scope:ec_state_1
															this = scope:ec_state_2
															this = scope:ec_state_3
															this = scope:ec_state_4
														}
														save_temporary_scope_as = ec_state_5
														owner = root
														OR = {
															has_building = building_port
															any_neighbouring_state = {
																NOR = {
																	this = scope:ec_state_1
																	this = scope:ec_state_2
																	this = scope:ec_state_3
																	this = scope:ec_state_4
																	this = scope:ec_state_5
																}
																owner = root
																has_building = building_port
															}
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						root = {
							add_to_variable_list = {
								name = ec_safe_to_remove_ports_in_outer_lands
								target = prev
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Calculate free workforce that is available in the state
		
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_available_workforce
			value = ec_unemployed_population
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_pop = {
					is_pop_type = peasants
					OR = {
						pop_employment_building_group =	bg_subsistence_agriculture
						pop_employment_building_group =	bg_subsistence_ranching
					}
				}
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
			every_scope_building = {
				limit = {
					is_subsistence_building = yes
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_available_workforce
						add = {
							value = prev.level
							multiply = 10000
							multiply = prev.occupancy
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Set up state level counters of government building
		
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_government_administration_level
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_construction_sector_level
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_university_level
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_railway_level
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_port_level
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_barracks_level
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_naval_base_level
			value = 0
		}
		
		# Cycle through every building and count government ones on both country and state level
		
		save_scope_as = ec_current_state
		every_scope_building = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_government_administration
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_government_administration_count
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_government_administration_level
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_construction_sector
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_construction_sector_count
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_construction_sector_level
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_university
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_university_count
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_university_level
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_railway
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_railway_count
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_railway_level
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_port
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_port_count
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_port_level
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_barracks
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_barracks_count
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_barracks_level
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_building_type = building_naval_base
				}
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_naval_base_count
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
				scope:ec_current_state = {
					change_variable = {
						name = ec_naval_base_level
						add = prev.level
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_saved_scope = ec_current_state
		
		# Check if the state contains any excess production
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				root = {
					has_variable = ec_check_excess_production
				}
				#NOT = { has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce }
			}
			ec_check_excess_production_on_state_level = yes
		}
		
		# Check if the state meets requirements of being suitable for building
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ec_infrastructure_load_percent >= 0.90
					AND = {
						ec_infrastructure_load_value >= -15
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_railway
							is_under_construction = yes
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce
					has_variable = cbheb
				}
			}
			root = {
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ec_suitable_states_1
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ec_infrastructure_load_percent >= 0.70
				OR = {
					has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce
					has_variable = cbheb
				}
			}
			root = {
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ec_suitable_states_2
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ec_infrastructure_load_percent >= 0.70
			}
			root = {
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ec_suitable_states_3
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce
					has_variable = cbheb
				}
			}
			root = {
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = ec_suitable_states_4
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}
		remove_variable = cbheb
	}
	
	# Clear excess production variables
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			root = {
				has_variable = ec_check_excess_production
			}
		}
		ec_clear_excess_production_variables = yes
	}
}

### DOWNSIZING OF EXCESS GOVERNMENT AND PRODUCTION BUILDINGS

ec_downsize_excess_buildings = {
	
	# Government administration
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				bureaucracy >= ec_bureaucracy_ceiling
				AND = {
					bureaucracy >= ec_bureaucracy_excess
					any_scope_state = {
						percent <= 0.15
						ec_tax_capacity_load_percent < 1.10
					}
				}
			}
			any_scope_state = { has_building = building_government_administration }
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_government_administration
					level >= 1
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
				NOT = {
					root = {
						any_scope_state = {
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_government_administration
								level >= 1
							}
							var:ec_government_administration_level < ec_current_government_administration_level
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
					ec_government_administration_downsizing_threshold >= ec_current_government_administration_level
				}
				remove_building = building_government_administration
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Construction sector
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = 0
						}
					}
					OR = {
						modifier:country_construction_add >= ec_construction_points_excess
						ec_construction_costs_value > ec_construction_costs_excess
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -2
						}
					}
					OR = {
						modifier:country_construction_add >= ec_construction_points_target
						ec_construction_costs_value > ec_construction_costs_target
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -4
						}
					}
					ec_is_using_military_forces = no
				}
			}
			any_scope_state = { has_building = building_construction_sector }
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_construction_sector
					level >= 1
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
				NOT = {
					root = {
						any_scope_state = {
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_construction_sector
								level >= 1
							}
							var:ec_construction_sector_level < ec_current_construction_sector_level
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						root = {
							NOT = {
								ec_budget_health = {
									level = -4
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
							ec_construction_sector_downsizing_threshold >= ec_current_construction_sector_level
						}
					}
				}
				remove_building = building_construction_sector
			}
		}
	}
	
	# University
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = 0
						}
					}
					OR = {
						modifier:country_weekly_innovation_add >= ec_innovation_excess
						ec_university_count >= ec_university_excess
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -1
						}
					}
					OR = {
						modifier:country_weekly_innovation_add >= ec_innovation_target
						ec_university_count >= ec_university_target
						var:ec_government_costs >= ec_government_costs_ceiling
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -2
						}
					}
					var:ec_government_costs >= ec_government_costs_excess
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -3
						}
					}
					var:ec_government_costs >= ec_government_costs_target
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -4
						}
					}
					ec_is_using_military_forces = no
				}
			}
			any_scope_state = { has_building = building_university }
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_university
					level >= 1
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
				NOT = {
					root = {
						any_scope_state = {
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_university
								level >= 1
							}
							var:ec_university_level < ec_current_university_level
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						root = {
							NOT = {
								ec_budget_health = {
									level = -4
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
							ec_university_downsizing_threshold >= ec_current_university_level
						}
					}
				}
				remove_building = building_university
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Railway
	
	# Port
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = 0
						}
					}
					ec_convoys_current >= ec_convoys_ceiling
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -1
						}
					}
					OR = {
						ec_convoys_current >= ec_convoys_excess
						var:ec_government_costs >= ec_government_costs_ceiling
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -2
						}
					}
					OR = {
						ec_convoys_current >= ec_convoys_target
						var:ec_government_costs >= ec_government_costs_excess
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -3
						}
					}
					var:ec_government_costs >= ec_government_costs_target
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -4
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						any_scope_building = {
							OR = {
								is_building_type = building_construction_sector
								is_building_type = building_university
							}
						}
					}
					ec_is_using_military_forces = no
				}
			}
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_port
				OR = {
					root = {
						NOR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable_list = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
								variable_list_size = {
									name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
									value > 0
								}
							}
							any_country = {
								market.owner = root
								any_scope_state = {
									is_coastal = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
					root = {
						is_target_in_variable_list = {
							name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
							target = prev
						}
						any_in_list = {
							variable = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
							count > 1
							has_building = building_port
						}
					}
					root = {
						is_target_in_variable_list = {
							name = ec_safe_to_remove_ports_in_outer_lands
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_port
				OR = {
					root = {
						NOR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable_list = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
								variable_list_size = {
									name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
									value > 0
								}
							}
							any_country = {
								market.owner = root
								any_scope_state = {
									is_coastal = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
					root = {
						is_target_in_variable_list = {
							name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
							target = prev
						}
						any_in_list = {
							variable = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
							count > 1
							has_building = building_port
						}
					}
					root = {
						is_target_in_variable_list = {
							name = ec_safe_to_remove_ports_in_outer_lands
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
				NOT = {
					root = {
						any_scope_state = {
							has_building = building_port
							OR = {
								root = {
									NOR = {
										AND = {
											has_variable_list = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
											variable_list_size = {
												name = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
												value > 0
											}
										}
										any_country = {
											market.owner = root
											any_scope_state = {
												is_coastal = yes
											}
										}
									}
								}
								root = {
									is_target_in_variable_list = {
										name = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
										target = prev
									}
									any_in_list = {
										variable = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
										count > 1
										has_building = building_port
									}
								}
								root = {
									is_target_in_variable_list = {
										name = ec_safe_to_remove_ports_in_outer_lands
										target = prev
									}
								}
							}
							var:ec_port_level < ec_current_port_level
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						root = {
							NOT = {
								ec_budget_health = {
									level = -4
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
							ec_port_downsizing_threshold >= ec_current_port_level
						}
					}
				}
				remove_building = building_port
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Barracks
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			ec_is_using_military_forces = no
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = 0
						}
					}
					var:ec_barracks_count >= ec_battalions_ceiling
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -1
						}
					}
					OR = {
						var:ec_barracks_count >= ec_battalions_excess
						ec_military_costs_value >= ec_military_costs_ceiling
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -2
						}
					}
					OR = {
						var:ec_barracks_count >= ec_battalions_target
						ec_military_costs_value >= ec_military_costs_excess
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -3
						}
					}
					ec_military_costs_value >= ec_military_costs_target
				}
				NOT = {
					ec_budget_health = {
						level = -4
					}
				}
			}
			var:ec_barracks_count >= ec_battalions_threshold
			any_scope_state = { has_building = building_barracks }
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_barracks
					level >= 1
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
				NOT = {
					root = {
						any_scope_state = {
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_barracks
								level >= 1
							}
							var:ec_barracks_level < ec_current_barracks_level
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
					ec_barracks_downsizing_threshold >= ec_current_barracks_level
				}
				remove_building = building_barracks
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Naval base
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			ec_is_using_military_forces = no
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = 0
						}
					}
					navy_size >= ec_flotillas_ceiling
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -1
						}
					}
					OR = {
						navy_size >= ec_flotillas_excess
						ec_military_costs_value >= ec_military_costs_ceiling
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -2
						}
					}
					OR = {
						navy_size >= ec_flotillas_target
						ec_military_costs_value >= ec_military_costs_excess
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						ec_budget_health = {
							level = -3
						}
					}
					ec_military_costs_value >= ec_military_costs_target
				}
				NOT = {
					ec_budget_health = {
						level = -4
					}
				}
			}
			navy_size >= ec_flotillas_threshold
			any_scope_state = { has_building = building_naval_base }
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_naval_base
					level >= 1
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
				NOT = {
					root = {
						any_scope_state = {
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_naval_base
								level >= 1
							}
							var:ec_naval_base_level < ec_current_naval_base_level
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state
					ec_naval_base_downsizing_threshold >= ec_current_naval_base_level
				}
				remove_building = building_naval_base
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = ec_check_excess_production
		}
		ec_downsize_excess_production_buildings = yes
	}
}

### CLEAR VARIABLES USED IN DOWNSIZING BUT NOT IN BUILDING

ec_clear_downsize_variables = {
	remove_variable = ec_government_administration_count
	remove_variable = ec_construction_sector_count
	remove_variable = ec_railway_count
	remove_variable = ec_port_count
	remove_variable = ec_naval_base_count
	every_scope_state = {
		remove_variable = ec_government_administration_level
		remove_variable = ec_university_level
		remove_variable = ec_railway_level
		if = {
			limit = {
				root = {
					NOT = {
						has_variable = ec_check_excess_production
					}
					has_variable = ec_had_excess_production
				}
			}
			ec_clear_had_excess_production = yes
		}
	}
}

### CHECK CONSTRUCTION POINTS PER BUILDING AND FREE ONES

ec_check_construction_points = {
	
	#count them as state average?
	#set_variable = {
	#	name = ec_average_construction_efficiency
	#	value = 0
	#}
	#set_variable = {
	#	name = ec_amount_of_states
	#	value = 0
	#}
	#every_scope_state = {
	#	root = {
	#		change_variable = {
	#			name = ec_average_construction_efficiency
	#			add = prev.modifier:state_construction_mult
	#		}
	#		change_variable = {
	#			name = ec_amount_of_states
	#			add = 1
	#		}
	#	}
	#}
	
	# Calculate construction points needed for full speed progression of one building
	
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_construction_points_per_building
		value = {
			value = define:NEconomy|MAX_WEEKLY_CONSTRUCTION_PROGRESS
			divide = {
				value = 1
				add = modifier:state_construction_mult
				min = 0.01
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Calculate free construction points available for the country
	
	set_variable = {
		name = ec_free_construction_points
		value = {
			
			# Base value is how much construction country does have
			
			value = modifier:country_construction_add
			
			# If you are not deep in debt then add standard building limit over it to build a bit more and thus reduce downtime
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					scaled_debt <= 0.30
				}
				add = {
					value = ec_building_limit_standard
					multiply = {
						value = var:ec_construction_points_per_building
						min = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			
			# If you are deep in debt then instead only part of queue potential is used to reduce construction costs
			
			else = {
				multiply = {
					value = 0.55 # from 0.30 to 0.50
					subtract = scaled_debt
					multiply = 4
					min = 0.20
					max = 1.00
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Can't beat vanilla AI otherwise
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:ec_free_construction_points < ec_points_for_three_buildings
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ec_free_construction_points
			value = ec_points_for_three_buildings
		}
	}
	
	# Subtract construction points that are already used for buildings in the queue
	
	change_variable = {
		name = ec_free_construction_points
		subtract = {
			value = num_queued_constructions
			multiply = {
				value = var:ec_construction_points_per_building
				min = 0.5
			}
		}
	}
}

### CHECK AND CONSTRUCT SPECIAL BUILDINGS SUCH AS MONUMENTS OR CANALS

ec_construct_special_buildings = {
	
	# Suez Canal
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = colonization
			owns_treaty_port_in = STATE_SINAI
			has_variable = suez_survey_complete
			NOT = {
				s:STATE_SINAI = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_suez_canal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_SINAI = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_suez_canal
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Panama Canal
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = civilizing_mission
			owns_treaty_port_in = STATE_PANAMA
			has_variable = panama_survey_complete
			NOT = {
				s:STATE_PANAMA = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_panama_canal
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_PANAMA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_panama_canal
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Big Ben
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			s:STATE_HOME_COUNTIES = {
				any_scope_state = {
					owner = root
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_big_ben
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_HOME_COUNTIES = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_big_ben
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Eiffel Tower
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = steel_frame_buildings
			s:STATE_ILE_DE_FRANCE = {
				any_scope_state = {
					owner = root
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_eiffel_tower
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_ILE_DE_FRANCE = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_eiffel_tower
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Statue of Liberty
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_technology_researched = steel_frame_buildings
			s:STATE_NEW_YORK = {
				any_scope_state = {
					owner = root
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_statue_of_liberty
					}
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_NEW_YORK = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = root
				}
				start_building_construction = building_statue_of_liberty
			}
		}
	}
}

### CLEARING VARIABLES THAT ARE USED GLOBALLY

# Country level variables with additional values

ec_clear_country_variables = {
	remove_variable = ec_incorporated_population
	remove_variable = ec_coastal_incorporated_population
	remove_variable = ec_incorporated_gdp
	remove_variable = ec_previous_gold_reserves
	remove_variable = ec_previous_debt
	remove_variable = ec_country_weekly_surplus
	ec_clear_budget_cost_variables = yes
}

# Building variables with all the data used in evaluation and constructing

ec_clear_building_variables = {
	
	remove_variable = ec_square_root_of_incorporated_population
	remove_variable = ec_square_root_of_construction_points
	remove_variable = ec_square_root_of_gdp
	remove_variable = ec_square_root_of_gdp_per_capita
	remove_variable = ec_square_root_of_incorporated_gdp_per_capita
	remove_variable = ec_square_root_of_minus_half_unincorporated_gdp_per_capita
	remove_variable = ec_surplus_bureaucracy_target
	
	remove_variable = ec_lowest_infrastructure
	remove_variable = ec_lowest_tax_capacity
	
	clear_variable_list = ec_coastline_of_market_capital
	clear_variable_list = ec_coastline_of_outer_lands
	clear_variable_list = ec_safe_to_remove_ports_in_outer_lands
	
	# Variables from downsizing that are used in building as well
	
	remove_variable = ec_university_count
	remove_variable = ec_barracks_count
	
	remove_variable = ec_had_excess_production
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = ec_check_excess_production
		}
		remove_variable = ec_check_excess_production
		set_variable = ec_had_excess_production
	}
	
	clear_variable_list = ec_suitable_states_1
	clear_variable_list = ec_suitable_states_2
	clear_variable_list = ec_suitable_states_3
	clear_variable_list = ec_suitable_states_4
	
	remove_variable = ec_construction_points_per_building
	remove_variable = ec_free_construction_points
	
	remove_variable = ec_building_days
	
	ec_clear_technicals = yes
	every_scope_state = {
		remove_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce
		remove_variable = ec_available_workforce
		remove_variable = ec_construction_sector_level
		remove_variable = ec_port_level
		remove_variable = ec_barracks_level
		remove_variable = ec_naval_base_level
		remove_variable = cbqab
	}
}

### DECHIPER ecpar

ec_decipher_ecpar = {
	set_variable = {
		name = ecpar
		value = state_region.var:ecpar
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ecpar1
		value = var:ecpar
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 300000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 300000
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 200000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 200000
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 100000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 100000
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ecpar2
		value = var:ecpar
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 30000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 30000
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 20000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 20000
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 10000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 10000
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ecpar3
		value = var:ecpar
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 3000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 3000
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 2000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 2000
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 1000
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 1000
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ecpar4
		value = var:ecpar
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 300
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 300
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 200
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 200
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 100
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 100
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ecpar5
		value = var:ecpar
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 30
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 30
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 20
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 20
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			var:ecpar >= 10
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = ecpar
			subtract = 10
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		name = ecpar6
		value = var:ecpar
	}
	remove_variable = ecpar
}

### BUILDING CODE GENERATED BY OUTSIDE SCRIPT

ec_create_identifying_object_list = { clear_global_variable_list = cbiol every_state_region = { if = { limit = { has_variable = cbiob } remove_variable = cbiob } if = { limit = { has_variable = cbpor } remove_variable = cbpor } } set_variable = { name = cbiob value = 1 } while = { limit = { var:cbiob <= ec_amount_of_building_types } random_state_region = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = cbiob } } add_to_global_variable_list = { name = cbiol target = this } set_variable = { name = cbiob value = prev.var:cbiob } if = { limit = { var:cbiob = 1 } set_variable = { name = cbpor value = 1 } } ec_add_building_to_priority_list = {

target = scope:ec_current_building } } else_if = { limit = { var:$cber$ = 3 } add_to_variable_list = { name = cbbp3 target = scope:ec_current_building } } else_if = { limit = { var:$cber$ = 4 } yes has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce } root = { add_to_variable_list = { name = cbb1o1 target = prev } } } else_if = { limit = { is_incorporated = no has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce } root = { add_to_variable_list = { name = cbb1o2 target = prev } } } else_if = { limit = { is_incorporated = yes NOT = { has_variable = ec_state_has_free_workforce } } ec_current_state random_scope_building = { limit = { is_building_type = building_government_administration } if = { limit = { level <= 0 is_under_construction = yes } scope:ec_current_state = { set_variable = { name = cbcbl value = 1 } } } else = { scope:ec_current_state = { set_variable = { name = cbcbl value = { value = prev.level min = 1 } } change_variable = { name = cbcbl multiply = { value = prev.occupancy min = 0 max = 1 } } } } } clear_saved_scope = ec_current_state } } while = { limit = { has_variable_list = cbcpl variable_list_size = { name = cbcpl value > 0 } var:cbb1c < ec_building_limit_adjusted } random_in_list = { variable = cbcpl limit = { save_temporary_scope_as = ec_current_state root = { NOT = { any_in_list = { variable = cbcpl var:cbcbl < ec_current_cbcbl } } set_variable = { name = cbcbl value = 1 } } } else = { scope:ec_current_state = { change_variable = { name = cbcbl add = { value = prev.occupancy min = 0.01 } } } } } clear_saved_scope = ec_current_state root = { change_variable = { name = cbb1c add = 1 } } } else = { remove_variable = cbcbl root = { remove_list_variable = { name = cbcpl target = prev } } } remove_variable = cbnqc } }
